# I-complete-001 (#1182) — combined DIFF gate: 3 completeness fixes

You are reviewing a single combined diff that implements three independent completeness fixes (D-1, D-5, D-2) found in the I-ready-017 / beat-both forensic audit. The umbrella goal of I-complete-001 is to close COMPLETENESS gaps (POLARIS dropping/under-counting content vs Gemini/ChatGPT) WITHOUT fabricating any content and WITHOUT weakening any faithfulness gate.

VERIFY EACH FIX INDEPENDENTLY against the diff below. Do not assume; read the code. Reserve P0/P1 for real execution/faithfulness risks.

## Hard constraints (faithfulness — non-negotiable; flag P0 if any is violated)
- No fix may weaken `strict_verify`, the 4-role verifier, the redactor, or the FX-01 reasoning->content promotion guard (which REFUSES to ship a model's reasoning scratchpad as content).
- No fix may fabricate quantified or narrative content.
- No magic numbers (LAW VI): every threshold/budget must be a named, env-overridable constant or named module constant.
- Metadata-honesty fixes (D-5) must change ONLY counts/disclosure, never generated prose.

## Fix-by-fix summary (what to verify)

### D-1 — content max_tokens raised via a named env-overridable constant
Files: `src/polaris_graph/generator/multi_section_generator.py`, `src/polaris_graph/generator/analyst_synthesis.py`.
- The prior hardcoded content ceilings (`4000` in analyst-synthesis, `2400`/`4000` in multi-section, `6000` contract-slot floor) are replaced with named module constants `PG_SECTION_MAX_TOKENS` (default 24000) and `PG_CONTRACT_SLOT_MIN_MAX_TOKENS` (default 6000), both `os.getenv`-overridable.
- Rationale: the default writer (deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro) is REASONING-FIRST; it burns 6k-42k reasoning tokens before content, so a small content ceiling caused finish_reason=length truncation, after which the FX-01 guard correctly REFUSED the scratchpad and DROPPED whole sections (a completeness loss).
- VERIFY: (a) the truncation GUARD itself is UNTOUCHED (the diff only widens the requested budget, it does NOT disable the refusal-to-ship-scratchpad guard); (b) no magic number remains for content budget; (c) faithfulness untouched.

IMPORTANT NUANCE TO ADJUDICATE (do not let me pre-judge this; you decide if it is a blocker):
`openrouter_client` clamps every reasoning-first request: it FLOORS UP requests below `PG_REASONING_FIRST_MIN_MAX_TOKENS` (default 16384) and CLAMPS DOWN requests above `PG_REASONING_FIRST_HARD_CAP` (default 16384). The relevant code is pasted at the bottom under "EVIDENCE: openrouter clamp". Consequence on the DEFAULT provider: a reasoning-first content call receives 16384 whether the kwarg is the old 4000 or the new 24000 — i.e. for the reasoning-first content sites, D-1 may be a NO-OP on the deployed default config, taking effect only once an operator points the writer at a higher-tier endpoint AND raises `PG_REASONING_FIRST_HARD_CAP`. The diff comments openly concede this ("forward-compat HEADROOM, not active room"). The OPEN QUESTIONS for you:
  1. Is D-1 effectively a no-op on the default provider at the reasoning-first content sites (analyst-synthesis call, per-section call, section signature default)? Trace whether each of those calls enables reasoning and hits the clamp branch. NOTE the old hardcoded 4000 was ALSO below the 16384 floor, so it too was floored up to 16384 — meaning the *effective* budget on the default provider may be UNCHANGED by D-1 at those sites.
  2. Does the contract-slot site `max(section_max_tokens, PG_CONTRACT_SLOT_MIN_MAX_TOKENS)` behave any differently (e.g. non-reasoning or JSON path) such that D-1 DOES change effective budget there?
  3. Given the above, does "forward-compat headroom only" satisfy the COMPLETENESS intent of I-complete-001 D-1, or is the real fix elsewhere (e.g. the operator must also raise PG_REASONING_FIRST_HARD_CAP, or the writer must be pointed at a higher endpoint)? Decide whether shipping D-1 as-is (named constant + headroom + honest comments) is acceptable, or whether it is a P1 "claims to fix truncation but is inert on the deployed config." It is your call, not mine.

### D-5 — sections_kept count excludes 0-verified gap stubs (metadata honesty)
Files: `scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py` (3 sites: strict_verify.section_completed `global` flag, Methods parallel-section count, manifest `generator.sections_kept`) + NEW UNTRACKED FILE `.codex/beatboth5/build_forensic_input.py` (D-5 consumer disclosure).
- A 0-verified gap stub ships `dropped_due_to_failure=False` with non-empty disclosure `verified_text` and `sentences_verified=0`. The OLD count (`not dropped_due_to_failure`) therefore counted gap stubs as kept/verified sections, inflating POLARIS's section count vs Gemini/ChatGPT on the §-1.1 beat-both surface.
- The fix replaces the bare not-dropped check with the UNIVERSAL SURVIVOR SIGNAL: `not dropped_due_to_failure and not getattr(s, "is_gap_stub", False) and getattr(s, "sentences_verified", 1) > 0`.
- VERIFY: (a) this is the SAME survivor signal already used by the existing consumer `key_findings.py` (which skips when `is_gap_stub or sentences_verified == 0`) — confirm semantic equivalence so the count matches what already renders as verified prose; (b) the change is METADATA-ONLY (counts + disclosure), no generated content changes; (c) the `getattr(..., 1)` default of 1 is safe for objects predating the attribute (i.e. a real section without the attr is NOT wrongly excluded); (d) all three run_honest_sweep_r3.py sites + build_forensic_input use the same signal consistently.
- NOTE: `.codex/beatboth5/build_forensic_input.py` is an UNTRACKED new file (will NOT appear in `git diff`). Its D-5 region is pasted in full below under "EVIDENCE: build_forensic_input.py (untracked, D-5 region)". Review it there.

### D-2 — quantified differentiator no-op is LOUD, not a fabricated fix
Files: `src/polaris_graph/generator/quantified_analysis.py`, `tests/polaris_graph/synthesis/test_quantified_tradeoff_phase7.py`.
- This is a DOCUMENTED, LOUD instrumentation change — NOT a forced fix and NOT fabricated quantified content. It adds a single-field `telem["firing_status"]` set at EVERY return point of `run_quantified_section`, so a `spec_produced=False` / `fired=False` manifest names WHERE the differentiator died instead of being silent.
- Distinct statuses: `started` (default), `spec_provider_error` (Writer/transport raised), `no_spec_returned` (spec_provider returned non-dict — caller collapses transport-failure AND legitimate decline into None, so this status is honestly ambiguous), `spec_validation_rejected` (dict failed build_quantified_spec), `execution_failed` (sandbox), `no_verified_sentences` (Regime C dropped all), `fired` (landed).
- VERIFY: (a) this introduces NO fabricated content — `firing_status` is pure telemetry, the `return None, telem` early-exits are unchanged in control flow (no path that previously returned None now returns a section, and vice versa); (b) the consumer `quantified_degradation_disclosure` in run_honest_sweep_r3.py already reads `telemetry.get("firing_status")` so this is wiring a previously-unpopulated field, not inventing a surface; (c) the `no_spec_returned` comment honestly concedes ambiguity rather than guessing a confident reason; (d) tests assert each status path.

## Cross-cutting checks (flag P0/P1 if violated)
- No fix weakens strict_verify / 4-role verifier / redactor / FX-01 promotion guard.
- No faithfulness regression anywhere.
- All new constants are named + env-overridable (LAW VI).
- D-5 is metadata-only; D-2 is telemetry-only; neither alters generated prose.

## Known minor (already classified P3 by me; confirm or downgrade)
- `multi_section_generator.py` line ~4842: a DOCSTRING still says "default section_max_tokens=2400 budget" — stale documentation drift now that the default is `PG_SECTION_MAX_TOKENS` (24000). Comment-only, not active code. P3 doc-nit.

## Smoke evidence
- `tests/polaris_graph/synthesis/test_quantified_tradeoff_phase7.py`: 32 passed (incl. 3 new D-2 firing_status tests + the existing end-to-end `fired` assertion).

```python
    # generator
    # D-5 (#1182): sections_kept is the POLARIS section count surfaced into the §-1.1
    # POLARIS-vs-Gemini/ChatGPT comparison. As of the D-5 fix, run_honest_sweep_r3.py
    # computes sections_kept EXCLUDING 0-verified gap stubs (the universal survivor
    # signal: not dropped_due_to_failure and not is_gap_stub and sentences_verified>0),
    # so this count no longer over-states POLARIS's verified section count. Manifests
    # produced BEFORE the D-5 fix may carry a stale-inflated sections_kept; the manifest
    # lacks per-section is_gap_stub / sentences_verified, so the corrected count can only
    # be re-derived by re-running the sweep on the fixed code (not recomputed here).
    lines.append("\n### generator")
    lines.append(
        "- (D-5 #1182: sections_kept EXCLUDES 0-verified gap stubs ONLY for manifests "
        "generated AFTER the D-5 fix landed; manifests generated BEFORE the fix may "
        "OVER-COUNT sections by including gap stubs, and that over-count cannot be "
        "corrected here — the manifest carries no per-section is_gap_stub / "
        "sentences_verified, so re-derivation requires re-running the sweep on fixed code.)"
    )
    for k in ['sections_kept','sentences_verified','sentences_dropped','verified_words','words','limitations_words','analyst_synthesis_words','analyst_synthesis_input_tokens','analyst_synthesis_output_tokens']:
        lines.append(f"- {k}: {g(m,'generator',k)}")
    lines.append(f"- outline_sections: {fmt(g(m,'generator','outline_sections'),300)}")
```

This is a read-only DISCLOSURE/annotation in the forensic-input builder — it does NOT recompute the count, it annotates that the count's meaning changed after the D-5 fix. Confirm it is purely additive disclosure (no recompute, no content change) and that the survivor-signal description it states matches the run_honest_sweep_r3.py implementation above.

## EVIDENCE: openrouter clamp (src/polaris_graph/llm/openrouter_client.py lines ~1680-1695) — for the D-1 nuance adjudication

```python
            # confirmed: at 20000, V4 Pro completed all 6 sections with
            # zero ReasoningFirstTruncationError.
            # I-bug-941 (#927): default LOWERED 20000 → 16384 to match DeepInfra's
            # deepseek-v4-pro provider cap (verified by binary search 2026-05-28: 16384
            # → 200, 16385 → 404 "No endpoints found"). Operators with higher-tier
            # endpoints can override via env. The 20000 floor produced a deterministic
            # 404 on every generation call against the default provider configuration.
            _min_tokens = int(os.getenv("PG_REASONING_FIRST_MIN_MAX_TOKENS", "16384"))
            if body.get("max_tokens", 0) < _min_tokens:
                body["max_tokens"] = _min_tokens
            # Hard ceiling at DeepInfra's verified cap for deepseek-v4-pro. The runner's
            # per-section/outline max_tokens kwargs can legally request higher (e.g. 24000
            # for V30 Phase-2 long-form sections); without this clamp those requests 404.
            _hard_cap = int(os.getenv("PG_REASONING_FIRST_HARD_CAP", "16384"))
            if body.get("max_tokens", 0) > _hard_cap:
                body["max_tokens"] = _hard_cap
```

1544:    async def _call(
1545:        self,
1546:        messages: list[dict[str, str]],
1547:        call_type: str,
1548:        reasoning_enabled: bool = True,
1549:        reasoning_effort: str = "high",
1550:        temperature: float = 0.7,
1551:        max_tokens: int = 16384,
1552:        response_format: Optional[dict] = None,
1553:        timeout: Optional[float] = None,
1554:        reasoning_max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
1555:        reasoning_exclude: Optional[bool] = None,
1556:    ) -> LLMResponse:
1557:        """Make a single API call to OpenRouter.
1558:
1559:        A8.2: Acquires global concurrency semaphore before executing.
1560:        This prevents GPU OOM on sovereign deployments and 429 rate
1561:        limits on cloud APIs by limiting parallel LLM calls.
1562:        """
1563:        # A8.2: Global concurrency control
1564:        from src.providers.llm_provider import get_semaphore
1565:        semaphore = get_semaphore()
1566:        async with semaphore:
1567:            return await self._call_impl(
1568:                messages, call_type, reasoning_enabled, reasoning_effort,
1569:                temperature, max_tokens, response_format, timeout,
1570:                reasoning_max_tokens, reasoning_exclude,
1571:            )
1572:
1573:    async def _call_impl(
1574:        self,
1575:        messages: list[dict[str, str]],
1576:        call_type: str,
1577:        reasoning_enabled: bool = True,
1578:        reasoning_effort: str = "high",
1579:        temperature: float = 0.7,
1580:        max_tokens: int = 16384,
1581:        response_format: Optional[dict] = None,
1582:        timeout: Optional[float] = None,
1583:        reasoning_max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
1584:        reasoning_exclude: Optional[bool] = None,
1585:    ) -> LLMResponse:
1586:        """Internal implementation — called within semaphore context."""
1587:        # FIX-402: Short-circuit all calls once 402 Payment Required is received.
1588:        if OpenRouterClient._billing_exhausted:
1589:            raise BillingExhaustedException(
1590:                "OpenRouter billing exhausted (402 circuit breaker OPEN). "
1591:                "No API calls will be attempted."
1592:            )
1593:
1594:        if self.usage.budget_exhausted:
1595:            raise BudgetExhaustedError(
1596:                f"Budget exhausted: ${self.usage.total_cost_usd:.2f} "
1597:                f">= ${self.usage.budget_usd:.2f}"
1598:            )
1599:
1600:        # R-2: check the shared per-run budget cap. Each client
1601:        # contributes to _RUN_COST_USD after each call; here we abort
1602:        # early if the cap is already breached rather than fire another
1603:        # call and discover the overage after the fact.
1604:        check_run_budget(anticipated_additional=0.0)
1605:
1606:        # K2-3: Filter reasoning_content: null from messages to prevent
1607:        # prompt pollution (literal "null" causes model confusion).

2944:    async def generate_structured(
2945:        self,
2946:        prompt: str,
2947:        schema: Type[T],
2948:        system: str = "",
2949:        max_tokens: int = 8192,
2950:        timeout: Optional[float] = None,
2951:        reasoning_enabled: bool = False,
2952:        reasoning_effort: str = "high",
2953:        reasoning_max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
2954:        reasoning_exclude: Optional[bool] = None,
2955:    ) -> T:
2956:        """
2957:        Structured output call — reasoning OFF by default, returns parsed schema.
2958:
2959:        When reasoning is DISABLED and PG_STRICT_JSON_SCHEMA=1 (default),
2960:        sends response_format with json_schema + strict:true to enforce
2961:        schema compliance at the provider level (Qwen 3.5 Plus supports this).
2962:
2963:        When reasoning is ENABLED, relies on prompt-based JSON extraction
2964:        because thinking + json_schema response_format are incompatible.
2965:
2966:        FIX-QM1: When reasoning IS explicitly enabled, checks both content
2967:        and reasoning_content for JSON (some models put JSON in reasoning).
2968:        """
2969:        # Use strict:true JSON schema when reasoning is disabled and env allows.
2970:        # Qwen3.5-Plus supports strict schema enforcement. Gate behind
2971:        # PG_STRICT_JSON_SCHEMA (default "1") for backwards compatibility.
2972:        # When reasoning is enabled, skip — thinking + json_schema are incompatible.
2973:        #
2974:        # FIX-GLM5-STRUCTURED (2026-04-12): For models in _ALWAYS_REASON_MODELS,
2975:        # reasoning is forced ON by _call() regardless of this parameter. Without
2976:        # this check, GLM 5.1 receives BOTH response_format=json_schema strict:true
2977:        # AND reasoning=enabled, which causes complex-schema calls (StormOutlinePlan,
2978:        # SourceAnalysisBatch, ReportOutline) to dump 17K+ chars of prose into
2979:        # reasoning_content with content="" (empty). Symptom in PG_TEST_090 trace:
2980:        # "Content empty for structured:StormOutlinePlan, reasoning has 17958 chars".
2981:        # The fix makes generate_structured aware that these models always reason,
2982:        # so it skips response_format and uses prompt-based JSON extraction (which

1865:        f"Write the {section.title} paragraph now, following the rules."
1866:    )
1867:
1868:    client = OpenRouterClient(model=model)
1869:    try:
1870:        # I-gen-004 (#496): tag this LLM call for the reasoning-trace sink
1871:        # (no-op unless a run-scoped collector is registered).
1872:        set_reasoning_call_context(
1873:            section=section.title,
1874:            call_type="regen" if tighter_retry else "section",
1875:            attempt_n=2 if tighter_retry else 1,
1876:            regen_reason="tighter_retry" if tighter_retry else None,
1877:        )
1878:        # I-gen-005 (#904) part of combined fix: cold temperature on retry
1879:        # for reasoning-first models. The original I-gen-003 HARD CONTRACT
1880:        # was stripped in cb7feaa3 because Smoke #3 ran it at default
1881:        # temperature (0.3) and got zero verified-sentence lift in 12
1882:        # retries. Cold temp (0.1) was never tried in that test.
1883:        _retry_temp = temperature
1884:        if tighter_retry:
1885:            from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import (
1886:                _REASONING_FIRST_MODELS,
1887:            )
1888:            if model in _REASONING_FIRST_MODELS:
1889:                _retry_temp = 0.1
1890:        response = await client.generate(
1891:            prompt=prompt,
1892:            system=system,
1893:            max_tokens=max_tokens,
1894:            temperature=_retry_temp,
1895:        )
1896:    except ReasoningFirstTruncationError as exc:
1897:        # I-gen-003: a reasoning-first model (DeepSeek V4 Pro) ran out
1898:        # of token budget mid-planning even at the 20000-token floor.
1899:        # Do NOT let this crash the whole run — return an empty draft.
1900:        # An empty section is handled honestly downstream: if every
1901:        # section ends empty the pipeline reports abort_no_verified_
1902:        # sections (a real verdict per §9.3), not a hard error_unexpected
1903:        # crash. Logged loud, not silent — the failure surfaces in the
1904:        # section telemetry and this WARNING.
1905:        logger.warning(
1906:            "[multi_section] %s: reasoning-first truncation on %s "
1907:            "(max_tokens=%d, tighter_retry=%s) — empty draft returned. "
1908:            "detail: %s",
1909:            section.title, model, max_tokens, tighter_retry, exc,
1910:        )
1911:        # Step 3b commit 3: return atom_catalog (empty here — no draft to validate)
1912:        return "", 0, 0, _section_atoms
1913:    finally:
1914:        if hasattr(client, "close"):
1915:            try:
1916:                await client.close()
1917:            except Exception:
1918:                pass
1919:
1920:    # Step 3b commit 3: 4-tuple return — atom_catalog is the
1921:    # section-filtered dict injected into the system prompt.

1923:        (response.content or "").strip(),
1924:        response.input_tokens,
1925:        response.output_tokens,
1926:        _section_atoms,
1927:    )

1934:
1935:# Trial short-name pattern. Generalizable across clinical trial programs —
---
1935:# Trial short-name pattern. Generalizable across clinical trial programs —
1936:# any ALL-CAPS token followed by a hyphen-digit suffix counts, plus a
1937:# small list of famous all-letters names. No drug-specific tokens.
1938:#
1939:# M-41c pass-2 (Codex audit medium #1): exclude standards-body /
1940:# engineering-identifier tokens that would false-positive match the
1941:# hyphen-digit pattern (ISO-9001, IEC-62109, DIN-17100, ASTM-D412,
1942:# ANSI-C, IEEE-754, NCT- prefixes, SAE-J series). These are technical
1943:# identifiers, not named clinical trials, and dropping sentences that
1944:# cite them would remove legitimate standards-mentioning prose.
1945:_M41C_TRIAL_NAME_DENYLIST: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
1946:    "ISO", "IEC", "DIN", "ASTM", "ANSI", "IEEE", "SAE", "EN", "BS",
1947:    "UL", "JIS", "GB", "CAS", "ICH", "OECD", "USP", "EP", "USC",
1948:    "CFR", "EU", "US", "UN", "WHO", "FDA", "EMA", "NCT",
1949:})
1950:
1951:_M41C_TRIAL_SHORT_NAME_RE = re.compile(
1952:    r"\b(?:"
1953:    r"[A-Z][A-Z0-9]{2,}-\d+(?:[A-Z]+)?"        # SURPASS-2, SURMOUNT-4, STEP-3
1954:    r"|[A-Z][A-Z0-9]{2,}-CVOT"                  # SURPASS-CVOT
1955:    r"|SELECT|LEADER|SUSTAIN|PIONEER|REWIND"    # famous all-letter names
1956:    r"|AWARD|GRADE|DEVOTE|HARMONY|CANVAS"
1957:    r"|DECLARE|EMPEROR"
1958:    r")\b",
1959:)
1960:
1961:
1962:# Frame-element detectors. A sentence is "framed" when it (or its
1963:# immediately preceding sentence) matches >=3 distinct classes.
1964:# Keep each class regex domain-agnostic; clinical-specific keywords
1965:# go in a permissive union with other-domain equivalents so the rule
1966:# generalizes beyond T2D trials.
1967:_M41C_FRAME_ELEMENT_PATTERNS: list[tuple[str, re.Pattern]] = [
1968:    (
1969:        "sample_size",
1970:        re.compile(
1971:            r"\bN\s*=\s*\d+\b"
1972:            r"|\b\d{2,}\s+(?:patients|participants|adults|subjects|"
1973:            r"enrolled|randomi[sz]ed|cases|samples|specimens)\b",
1974:            re.IGNORECASE,
1975:        ),
1976:    ),
1977:    (
1978:        "baseline",
1979:        re.compile(r"\bbaseline\b|\binitial\s+value\b", re.IGNORECASE),
1980:    ),
1981:    (
1982:        "comparator",
1983:        re.compile(
1984:            r"\b(?:vs|versus|compared\s+to|compared\s+with|"
1985:            r"against\s+placebo|non[-\s]inferior|superior\s+to|"
1986:            r"head[-\s]to[-\s]head|control\s+arm)\b",
1987:            re.IGNORECASE,
1988:        ),
1989:    ),
1990:    (
1991:        "dose_or_level",
1992:        re.compile(
1993:            r"\b\d+\.?\d*\s*(?:mg|mcg|µg|units|IU|kg|mmol|mol|nm|"
1994:            r"percent|wt%|ppm|mAh|MPa|GPa)\b",
1995:            re.IGNORECASE,
1996:        ),
1997:    ),
1998:    (
1999:        "endpoint",
2000:        re.compile(
2001:            r"\b(?:endpoint|primary\s+outcome|primary\s+efficacy|"
2002:            r"co-primary|key\s+secondary|HbA1c|body\s+weight|"
2003:            r"weight\s+loss|cardiovascular\s+outcome|MACE|cycle\s+life|"
2004:            r"capacity\s+retention|phase\s+transition|reaction\s+yield)\b",
2005:            re.IGNORECASE,
2006:        ),
2007:    ),
2008:    (
2009:        "timepoint",
2010:        re.compile(
2011:            r"\b(?:week|month|year|day)s?\s*\d+"
2012:            r"|\b\d+\s+(?:week|month|year|day)s?\b"
2013:            r"|\bat\s+(?:week|month|year)\s*\d+\b"
2014:            r"|\bover\s+\d+\s+(?:week|month|year)s?\b",
2015:            re.IGNORECASE,
2016:        ),
2017:    ),
2018:    (
2019:        "uncertainty",
2020:        re.compile(
2021:            r"p\s*[<>=]\s*0?\.\d+"                         # p<0.001
2022:            r"|\b\d+\s*%\s+CI\b"                           # 95% CI
2023:            r"|\bCI\s*[\(:]\s*"                            # CI (0.5 to 0.8)
2024:            r"|\b\(\s*\d+\.?\d*\s*(?:to|[-–])\s*\d+"       # (1.2 to 2.3)
2025:            r"|\bSD\s*\d|\bSE\s*\d"                        # SD 1.2
2026:            r"|±\s*\d",                                    # ±1.5
2027:            re.IGNORECASE,
2028:        ),
2029:    ),
2030:]

307:async def run_quantified_section(
308:    question: str,
309:    evidence_pool: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
310:    *,
311:    spec_provider,
312:    run_dir: str | None = None,
313:    credibility_analysis: Any = None,  # I-cred-008b (#1162): advisory per-claim disclosure; None => byte-identical
314:) -> tuple[str | None, dict[str, Any]]:
315:    """Sweep-facing orchestrator: Extract -> Model -> Execute -> Bind ->
316:    Verify(Regime C) -> verified "Quantified Trade-off" section.
317:
318:    ``spec_provider`` is an ASYNC callable ``(question, sourced_numbers) ->
319:    raw_spec_dict | None`` (the Writer in prod; a fake in tests) — the ONLY
320:    billed step, isolated here so the sync validation in ``build_quantified_spec``
321:    and the deterministic execute/verify stay spend-free-testable.
322:
323:    Returns ``(section_markdown | None, telemetry)``. The section is produced
324:    ONLY when a spec validates, executes, and at least one computed sentence
325:    survives Regime C.
326:    """
327:    from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (
328:        resolve_provenance_to_citations,
329:        strict_verify,
330:    )
331:    from src.polaris_graph.synthesis.tradeoff_modeler import build_quantified_spec
332:    from src.polaris_graph.tools.evidence_extractor import (
333:        extract_numbers_from_evidence,
334:    )
335:
336:    # FIX D-2 (#1182): ``firing_status`` is the LOUD, single-field reason the
337:    # quantified differentiator did or did not land — set at EVERY return point so a
338:    # ``spec_produced=False`` / ``fired=False`` manifest is never silent about WHERE it
339:    # died. The consumer ``quantified_degradation_disclosure`` (run_honest_sweep_r3.py)
340:    # already reads ``telemetry.get("firing_status")`` for its reader-facing disclosure,
341:    # but this producer never populated it — so a no-op surfaced only as a buried log.
342:    # Distinct values let a post-run audit tell "broken" (spec_provider_error /
343:    # execution_failed) apart from "legitimately inapplicable" (no_spec_returned with a
344:    # genuine Writer decline) without reading the raw log. Default = the pre-spec state.
345:    telem: dict[str, Any] = {
346:        "enabled": True, "spec_produced": False, "execution_success": False,
347:        "outputs": 0, "sourced_inputs": 0, "modeled_inputs": 0,
348:        "verified_sentences": 0, "dropped_sentences": 0, "conflicts": [],
349:        "firing_status": "started",
350:    }
351:
352:    sourced_numbers = extract_numbers_from_evidence(evidence_pool)
353:    telem["conflicts"] = detect_sourced_conflicts(sourced_numbers)
354:    telem["sourced_numbers_extracted"] = len(sourced_numbers)
355:
356:    try:
357:        raw_spec = await spec_provider(question, sourced_numbers)
358:    except Exception as exc:
359:        # UNAMBIGUOUSLY broken: the Writer/transport raised (e.g. a 404 on the
360:        # generator route surfaced as an exception). Loud, distinct, non-aborting.
361:        telem["firing_status"] = "spec_provider_error"
362:        telem["firing_error"] = str(exc)[:200]
363:        logger.warning(
364:            "[quantified_analysis] NO-OP (spec_provider_error): spec_provider raised: %s",
365:            str(exc)[:160],
366:        )
367:        return None, telem
368:    if not isinstance(raw_spec, dict):
369:        # AMBIGUOUS by construction: a prod ``spec_provider`` (the Writer closure in
370:        # run_honest_sweep_r3.py) collapses BOTH a transport failure (404 / empty 200 →
371:        # no JSON parsed) AND a legitimate Writer decline ({"model_id":"none"}) into a
372:        # bare ``None`` before it reaches us. We CANNOT tell broken from inapplicable
373:        # here — the caller lane must stop collapsing the two (see module summary). Tag
374:        # it honestly rather than guess a confident reason we can't support.
375:        telem["firing_status"] = "no_spec_returned"
376:        logger.warning(
377:            "[quantified_analysis] NO-OP (no_spec_returned): spec_provider returned "
378:            "no dict (transport failure OR legitimate Writer decline — caller collapses "
379:            "both into None; %d sourced numbers were available)",
380:            len(sourced_numbers),
381:        )
382:        return None, telem
383:
384:    spec = build_quantified_spec(
385:        question, sourced_numbers, evidence_pool,
386:        spec_llm=lambda _q, _s: raw_spec,
387:    )
388:    if spec is None:
389:        # The Writer returned a dict but it FAILED hard validation in
390:        # build_quantified_spec (datapoint identity, formula AST, material-dependency,
391:        # etc.). A defensible-but-rejected model, not a transport failure.
392:        telem["firing_status"] = "spec_validation_rejected"
393:        logger.warning(
394:            "[quantified_analysis] NO-OP (spec_validation_rejected): Writer emitted a "
395:            "spec dict but it failed build_quantified_spec validation (fail-closed)",
396:        )
397:        return None, telem
398:    telem["spec_produced"] = True
399:    telem["model_id"] = spec.model_id
400:    telem["sourced_inputs"] = len(spec.sourced_inputs)
401:    telem["modeled_inputs"] = len(spec.modeled_inputs)
402:
403:    result = await execute_quantified_model(spec, evidence_pool, run_dir=run_dir)
404:    if result is None:
405:        telem["firing_status"] = "execution_failed"
406:        logger.warning(
407:            "[quantified_analysis] NO-OP (execution_failed): spec validated but the "
408:            "deterministic sandbox execution did not return clean outputs (model %s)",
409:            spec.model_id,
410:        )
411:        return None, telem
412:    telem["execution_success"] = True
413:    telem["outputs"] = len(spec.outputs)
414:
415:    prose = render_decision_matrix_prose(spec, result)
416:    bound = bind_calc_tokens(prose, result)
417:    report = strict_verify(
418:        bound, evidence_pool, quantified_models={result.key(): result},
419:    )
420:    telem["verified_sentences"] = report.total_kept
421:    telem["dropped_sentences"] = report.total_dropped
422:    if report.total_kept == 0:
423:        # The spec executed but EVERY computed sentence failed Regime C (e.g. an
424:        # unlabeled modeled assumption, a number≠display mismatch). No verified prose.
425:        telem["firing_status"] = "no_verified_sentences"
426:        logger.warning(
427:            "[quantified_analysis] NO-OP (no_verified_sentences): %d computed "
428:            "sentence(s) all failed Regime C verification (model %s)",
429:            report.total_dropped, spec.model_id,
430:        )
431:        return None, telem
432:
433:    # I-cred-008b (#1162) SITE 4/4 (quantified trade-off): populate the advisory per-claim disclosure
434:    # on the kept SVs BEFORE resolve. This path returns (section_md, telem) — it has NO SectionResult,
435:    # so the populated SVs do NOT flow through kept_sentences_pre_resolve. To SURFACE them, we emit the
436:    # per-claim disclosure rows in `telem["claim_disclosure"]` (the runner merges them into
437:    # claim_disclosure.json). None => byte-identical (no populate, no telem key).
438:    if credibility_analysis is not None:
439:        from src.polaris_graph.synthesis.credibility_pass import apply_disclosure_to_svs
440:        report.kept_sentences = apply_disclosure_to_svs(
441:            report.kept_sentences, credibility_analysis,
442:        )
443:        telem["claim_disclosure"] = [
444:            {
445:                "sentence": getattr(_sv, "sentence", ""),
446:                "span_verdict": getattr(_sv, "span_verdict", ""),
447:                "credibility_weight": getattr(_sv, "credibility_weight", None),
448:                "independent_origin_count": getattr(_sv, "independent_origin_count", None),
449:                "certainty_label": getattr(_sv, "certainty_label", ""),
450:                "soft_warnings": list(getattr(_sv, "soft_warnings", None) or []),
451:            }
452:            for _sv in report.kept_sentences
453:        ]
454:
455:    # Reached only when a spec validated, executed, and ≥1 computed sentence survived
456:    # Regime C — the differentiator actually FIRED.
457:    telem["firing_status"] = "fired"
458:
459:    rendered, _biblio = resolve_provenance_to_citations(
460:        report.kept_sentences, evidence_pool,
461:    )
462:    section_md = f"### Quantified Trade-off\n\n{rendered}"
463:    return section_md, telem

**Findings**

P1: D-1 does not raise the section-writing budget on the primary sweep path. `run_honest_sweep_r3.py` still passes `section_max_tokens=int(os.environ.get("PG_SECTION_MAX_TOKENS", "5000"))`, which bypasses the new `generate_multi_section_report(... section_max_tokens=PG_SECTION_MAX_TOKENS)` default of `24000`. On the default DeepSeek path this is still floored/clamped to `16384`, so old/new are effectively unchanged; on a higher-cap endpoint, merely raising `PG_REASONING_FIRST_HARD_CAP` still leaves sweep section calls at the `16384` floor unless the operator also sets `PG_SECTION_MAX_TOKENS`. That means the main D-1 completeness fix is inert for legacy section prose in the deployed runner. See [scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py](C:/POLARIS/scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py:5558) and [src/polaris_graph/generator/multi_section_generator.py](C:/POLARIS/src/polaris_graph/generator/multi_section_generator.py:4510).

P2: D-2’s implementation covers all return statuses, but the tests do not assert every advertised status path. The added/updated tests cover `fired`, `no_spec_returned`, `spec_provider_error`, and `spec_validation_rejected`; I found no `firing_status` coverage for `execution_failed` or `no_verified_sentences`. This is a test gap, not a faithfulness/control-flow issue.

D-5 looks metadata-only and semantically aligned with `key_findings.py`: non-dropped, not `is_gap_stub`, and `sentences_verified > 0`, with the `getattr(..., 1)` default preserving older real section objects. The untracked forensic builder block is disclosure-only and does not recompute generated prose.

D-1 does not weaken FX-01 or strict verification; the clamp/guard path is untouched. The contract-slot call is also `client.generate()` on the default reasoning-first model, so it hits the same `16384` effective clamp; under the current sweep default it remains `max(5000, 6000)`, so it also does not gain the new `24000` headroom unless `PG_SECTION_MAX_TOKENS` is explicitly set.
